Page 13

Young Couple Suddenly Shot Dead in Shanfuli, Shanzhong Road: A Basket of Loquats Seemed to be a Gift Near the Dragon Boat Festival: The Sound of Gunshots Was Like a Group of Firecrackers, No One Cared:丨丨A Large Number of Banned Books in the Deceased's Room丨丨 167

At about 8:00 AM yesterday, a case of a young couple being shot and assassinated by thugs occurred in the pavilion room on the third floor of No. 64 Shanfuli, Lane 148 (i.e., Liujia Lane), Shanzhong Road, French Concession, behind the Gongshi Middle School (公時中學). Both died on the spot, and the perpetrators fled without a trace. The police heard the news and sent detectives to carry the two bodies to the mortuary for examination. The backgrounds of the two victims and the details of the murder are described below:

Young Couple 168

Liu Youqing, a native of Zhenjiang, was 38 years old and worked in the engineering department of the Shanghai Telephone Company. Several years ago, he acquired a three-story shikumen house at No. 84 Shanfuli, Lane 148, Shanzhong Road, and became a second landlord. He lived in the living room downstairs, and the remaining rooms were rented out to others. About a month and a half ago, a young couple living in No. 60 in the same neighborhood moved into Liu's pavilion room on the third floor with a young girl. The rent was set at six yuan per month. After the two parties agreed, they moved in immediately.

Evening Newspaper Translator 169

After this young couple moved in, they claimed that their names were Chen Fangruo, a native of Hubei, 28 years old, and the woman's name was Liu Jie, also a native of Hubei, 32 years old. The girl's name was Xiaolianzi, five years old. When asked where he worked, he said that he was a translator for the "大美晚報" (The Greater American Evening News). Liu saw that the couple were both literary and spoke very kindly, so he did not suspect anything else. After Chen moved in, the furnishings in the room were unusually simple, with only a half-bed, a writing desk, a rattan chair, four square stools, and a desk full of books, with nothing else of value.

Sudden Disaster 170

For three meals a day, the two cooked their own food. However, every day after 4:00 PM, Chen had to go out alone once, rain or shine, but the young woman never went out, and there were very few female visitors. Sometimes late at night, Chen still held a pen and wrote straight. The second landlord thought that Chen was in the newspaper industry and was probably writing at his desk, so he did not suspect anything else. Unexpectedly, at about 8:10 AM yesterday, Chen and his wife and daughter had all gotten up, and the girl was playing downstairs. Chen was sitting and reading the newspaper, and his wife was tidying up the bedclothes when the disaster suddenly struck.

Loquat Gift 171

At this moment, several thugs came to the back door of the house. Two people wearing black and white short clothes闯入 entered, while the rest remained outside. They pretended to be giving gifts. One person was carrying two bamboo baskets similar to loquats. When they entered the door, they asked where the Chen family lived. The second landlord replied that they lived in the pavilion room on the third floor. The two went straight upstairs. Not long after, more than a dozen gunshots were suddenly heard. At that time, the people downstairs initially suspected that the residents in the lane were setting off firecrackers, so they did not care.

Horrible Scene in the Room 172

Not long after, the child Xiaolianzi went upstairs for breakfast. She only saw that her parents had been shot dead in the room. She was extremely frightened and ran downstairs to tell the second landlord and his family the news. They rushed upstairs, but saw Chen still sitting dangerously on the chair, and Chen's wife was lying diagonally on the bed. Blood was flowing on the floor. They rushed to report to the police. The police chief sent Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. It was found that Chen Fangruo had been shot three times, one in the back of the neck, one in the brain, and one in the left eye socket, piercing through the right ear. His wife, Liu Jie, had been shot five times, one in the left hand fork, two bullets in the lip area, and two in the back, piercing through the front abdomen.

A Large Number of Books 173

The detectives saw that both people had died, so they immediately notified the Tongrenfuyuantang to send undertakers to carry the two bodies to the mortuary for examination. The detectives continued to carefully search the room. All the books were New Culture and various pamphlets that had been banned by the government. Then, according to the second landlord's statement, the detectives rushed to the 美晚報 (The Greater American Evening News) to investigate. The newspaper replied that there was no such person. After further investigation, they learned that Wu Youmei, the editor of the Zhonghua Daily Monthly, was on good terms with Chen. The detectives went to No. 67 Siming Village, Fuxu Road, to visit Wu.

Words of a Friend 174

When the detectives questioned Wu, Wu admitted that he was indeed friends with Chen and said that Chen was a graduate of Sun Yat-sen University in Moscow, Russia. Wu knew Chen from his student days. Chen's current situation was extremely difficult, and he only relied on submitting articles to make a living. He had recently published an article in the Labor Monthly, titled "The Second International Problem After Hitler Took Office". An article in the Zhonghua Daily was "The Restoration of Relations Between the United States and Russia," etc. According to Chen, he originally lived at No. 3 Sanheli, Xiaoshadu Road, at Dr. Li Guanying's residence, and then moved to No. 60 Shanfuli. A month and a half ago, he moved to No. 64. Wu did not want to say much after hearing the news of Chen's murder.

Corpse Examination 175

After the case occurred, the French Concession authorities paid special attention to it and ordered its subordinates to conduct a thorough investigation in order to get to the bottom of the case in the shortest possible time. The orphaned girl Xiaolianzi was temporarily raised by friends. Yesterday afternoon, the chief prosecutor Chen Beisan, along with forensic doctor Wei Ligong and clerk Zhao Yifen, came to the mortuary to examine the bodies on behalf of the Procuratorate of the Second Special District Court. It was verified that Chen's body had been hit by three bullets in the head, one entering from the left eyebrow and exiting from the upper corner of the left ear, one entering from the back of the head, and one entering from the top of the back of the head, none of which exited. Liu's body was hit by five bullets, two bullets entering from the back, piercing through the front chest, two entering from the upper and lower sides behind the left ear, one exiting from the left corner of the mouth, two teeth were knocked out, and one bullet passed through the fork between the index and middle fingers of the left hand. After the examination, the case was brought up in court. According to the report of the detective Zhang Chunsheng, the investigation was carried out after the incident. According to the testimony of Chen Wenfu (63 years old), a Ningbo native who was in charge of the alley, he witnessed the perpetrators entering and exiting. The official ruled that since no relatives of the deceased had arrived, it was verified that Chen Fangruo and Liu Jie had died from gunshot wounds during their lifetime. The bodies were temporarily handed over to Tongrenfuyuantang for burial, waiting for relatives to claim them and waiting for the police to arrest the perpetrators and bring them to justice. It is heard that the police have dispatched detectives to investigate the perpetrators in various directions.

French Yacht Arrives in Nagasaki 176

Creating a New Speed Record for Yachts to Japan: According to the Dalu Bao, the French yacht "迦白里爾 (Gablier) No. 2" of this port, 64 feet long and luxuriously decorated, set off for Japan on Sunday morning and arrived safely in Nagasaki at 10:30 AM yesterday, Thursday, creating a new speed record for yachts to Japan. This is two days faster than the German yacht "奇里登 (Chiridon)", which was 48 feet long at the time. The ship was piloted by French naval officer Biles and carried three French Municipal Council officials and two Chinese foremen. The yacht "丹那斯柯特 (Dunnscott)", which left Shanghai for Japan on the same day, piloted by the Danish Zhu Qinsheng, will probably take one or two more days to arrive in Nagasaki. However, this ship is the smallest yacht to ever go to Japan, only 27 feet long, so the speed is slower.

Ministry of Railways Contacts Banks in This City for Cold Storage Transportation Loans: Borrowed by Shanghai Bank and Others 181

According to the Shenshi News Agency, in order to improve the national railway transportation equipment, the Ministry of Railways decided to prepare for cold storage transportation on various routes. The entire project is divided into three phases, and the budget requires approximately 1.5 million yuan. The first phase requires approximately 500,000 yuan, which has been discussed by the Ministry of Railways with Shanghai Bank and others in this city for the supply of funds. A contract can be formally signed within days. The reporter of the Shenshi News Agency inquired about the situation as follows yesterday.

Cold Storage Transportation 182

In order to develop railway transportation and improve transportation facilities, the Ministry of Railways decided to implement the construction of national railway cold storage facilities to facilitate the transportation of various fresh fish, eggs, vegetables, fruits, and other goods. The total cost is 1.5 million yuan, and a plan has been formulated, divided into three phases: (1) The first phase will build cold storage facilities in Shanghai and Beijing, build ice stations in Hangzhou, and order ten ice storage vehicles, requiring a total of 560,000 yuan. (2) The second phase of the project will build cold storage facilities in Tianjin and Qingdao, set up four ice stations in Beiping, Jinan, Xuzhou, and Haizhou, and add two ice storage vehicles, requiring approximately 600,000 yuan. (3) The third phase of the project will build cold storage facilities in Guangzhou and Hankou, set up a foreign station in Wuchang, and add twelve cold storage vehicles, requiring 550,000 yuan.

Contact for Loans 183

In order to complete cold storage transportation, the Ministry of Railways decided to borrow the necessary funds from the banking sector in this city. The Ministry of Railways will designate a certain item of income as collateral, and then the funds will be repaid in installments from the income item. The Minister of Railways, Gu Mengyu, has come to Shanghai twice recently for this matter to contact the banking sector and determine the amount of the loan. It is estimated that Shanghai Bank will provide 500,000 yuan, China and other banks will provide a total of 500,000 yuan, and the remaining funds will be raised by the Ministry of Railways itself. According to inquiries made by the Shenshi News Agency reporter to Shanghai Bank yesterday, most of the details regarding the Ministry of Railways' loan have been agreed upon, but the amount is still somewhat flexible. After further consultation and determination, the loan contract can be formally signed within days.

Compilation and Publication of Series 185

Various countries have always attached importance to commercial statistics. In China, the one conducted by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce is the first of its kind. Initially, the association was limited by funds, and although it had been repeatedly resolved by the members' congresses in the past, it could not be held. Later, Executive Committee Member Luo Qinghua formulated a concrete plan and submitted it to the Executive Committee for approval before it could proceed in an orderly manner. It was decided that Luo would preside over the matter and invite nine leaders from various industries in this city, including Xu Jiqing, to organize a Business Committee to assist in everything. However, because this matter is of great importance and has many intricacies, the banking, money, trust, cotton, sugar, paper, coal, rice, silk, and yarn industries were selected as the first phase to start with. After three months of work, the banking, money, trust, and cotton industries have been completely completed and compiled into the Commercial Statistics Series for the reference of all sectors. The banking, money, and trust industries are compiled into one volume. Shanghai County Implements Work/Rest Bell 186

The Shanghai County Government, upon instruction from the Jiangsu Education Department, noting that in recent times, the populace in various regions has become accustomed to leisure and lacks a fixed schedule for work and rest, with a trend of late sleeping and late rising prevailing, especially in urban areas. In order to reform these habits, it was ordered to set up work/rest bells in cities and central locations of towns to alert and guide the people. The County Government designated the county seat location, utilizing the ancient bell of the Mingxin Temple at the North Bridge, as the work/rest bell. Now, the bell tower construction has been completed, and beginning the day before yesterday, a signal bell will be rung three times daily at fixed times in the morning, noon, and evening. County Head Pan has not only sent separate letters to inform everyone but also issued a public notice to all residents, so that all are aware.

Continued Statistics Collection 187

According to commercial statistics specialist Xue Guangqian of the New Voice News Agency, the first phase of statistics collection, besides the completed finance and cotton cloth industries, other industries are being actively processed and will soon be completed. It is now decided to select several more important industries in our country's industry and commerce, such as silk and woolen industries, electrical machinery and silk weaving factories, copper, iron and machine factories, etc., to continue planning surveys and conduct statistics, so as to clearly understand the true state of production and sales, and promote the development of industry and commerce. As for the formulation of investigation forms and the selection of statistical materials, preliminary designs have been made, and it is still necessary to invite leaders from various industries to study them to ensure thoroughness.

Li Shizeng Initiates Educational Savings Deposits; Entrusts Shanghai Trust Company to Handle 189

Mr. Li Shizeng of the World Society, in view of the fact that in recent years, students studying abroad often drop out due to insufficient tuition fees, which is deeply regrettable, initiated educational savings deposits so that there is adequate preparation beforehand, and they will not feel financially strained at the last minute. He discussed this idea with the Shanghai Trust Company, and the company formulated a plan in which the depositor budgets the amount needed and deposits a certain amount of principal at once. After that, the company will remit a fixed amount to the student on a regular basis to pay tuition fees. The deposit period will be determined according to needs, with the longest being monthly payments for as long as seven years. The interest rate is favorable, and the procedures are convenient. Yesterday, when the World Society sent off this year's students to the World School in Geneva, Mr. Li Shizeng invited the chairman of the company, Yang Jiemei, executive directors Guo Bingwen and Xu Jiying, and general and deputy managers, etc., to a tea party with the students' families, and announced this plan. The families of the students unanimously agreed, and each, according to their own situation and the required tuition fees, handed over the money to the company for deposit, and it will be remitted on schedule according to the regulations.

The Success of Chinese Reproduction of Car Tires 191

Yu Zhangtiankai, a giant in industry and commerce, a researcher in physics, chemistry, and mechanics, is excellent in learning and rich in perseverance. In the past, he used his experience to invent many kinds of electrical appliances and daily necessities, such as electric light bulb copper heads, etc. Famous electrical appliance factories all over the world competed to purchase them, and his reputation has long been known far and wide. Now, he has brought out his remaining energy to research artificial rubber and invented the reproduction of car tires, using discarded and useless old car tires, using scientific principles, to reproduce them into new ones, and they are strong, durable, and priced very cheaply. It is a gospel for those who own cars and operate transportation businesses. Therefore, as soon as the samples came out, people competed to buy them. When foreign merchants stationed in Shanghai heard the news, they frantically reduced the price of each tire, which used to sell for more than two hundred yuan, to the lowest price of more than one hundred yuan to compete. Inquiring about the car tire business, Chinese people have never manufactured or operated it, so it has always been arbitrarily manipulated by foreign merchants. Now, fortunately, reproduced car tires have been launched, so that foreign merchants cannot monopolize them. After being shocked, they have to lower prices to compete. It is a fact that our people have stopped leakage and recovered many rights and interests. It is heard that the factory has set up a new factory site on Robert Road, covering a large area, and has also set up a business department on Jiangxi Road, named China Tire Manufacturing Company, which has already started business. On the one hand, it has entrusted the Far East Company on Baker Road as its local manager, while the foreign manager is still being negotiated.

National Seaport Quarantine Administration Actively Carries Out Epidemic Prevention Work; Promotion and Vaccination Proceed Simultaneously; Plans to Establish Isolation and Epidemic Prevention Hospital 196

The National Seaport Quarantine Administration, with the summer season approaching and various infectious diseases expected to occur in due course, believes that if preventive measures are not taken in advance, it will not only have a direct impact on the citizens, but also have a profound impact on the public health of other areas. Therefore, it specially convened the health authorities of both the Chinese and foreign settlements in the city yesterday to discuss this year's cholera prevention methods, and plans to establish a hospital in the near future to treat various infectious diseases. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Prevention Meeting. The National Seaport Quarantine Administration convened a meeting yesterday for the sake of public health and safety in the city to discuss prevention strategies. Those present included Public Health Office representative Blahelaeh of the Public Concession's Municipal Council, Public Health Office representative Raduauate of the French Concession's Municipal Council, Municipal Health Bureau representative Cheng Muyi, and Seaport Quarantine Office representative Wu Changyao, etc., a total of more than ten people. The discussion began at 3 o'clock. As a result, it was decided that in addition to actively promoting and vaccinating, the investigation work will also be intensified to prevent the spread, and all major hospitals will be notified to report the patient status to the Chinese and foreign settlement health authorities on a daily basis for reference.

Planning and Establishing a Hospital. According to the person in charge of the office, the quarantine office has recently purchased eight mu of land near the Wusong Customs signal station for the purpose of preventing the spread of infectious diseases and providing practical diagnosis and treatment. It plans to build an isolation hospital to diagnose and treat various infectious diseases, including disinfection rooms, chemical testing rooms, libraries, staff dormitories, and other departments. As for the vicinity of the isolation hospital, a lookout post will be built to look out over passing ships and implement quarantine work. All work is limited to completion by the end of the year to benefit Chinese and foreign residents.

Drunk Man Pulls at Woman's Trousers 197

A Ningbo woman, Chen Xu, (29 years old) residing at No. 4, Jiaxiang Lane, Danfeng Road in the city, went to Xiaodongmen to buy clothing materials at 3:10 pm yesterday. When she reached the vicinity of the Dachang Silk Shop, a man came towards her and, without asking why, suddenly pulled down the woman's trousers, revealing her curves. As for pulling off Chen Xu's trousers while walking, it was indeed due to drunkenness. The section chief considered it related to public order and morals, and originally intended to hand him over to the bureau for severe handling, but because the defendant pleaded bitterly, he was leniently punished as a warning.

Suzhou Hotel Guest Commits Suicide by Taking Opium 198

A traveler came to the Suzhou Hotel at the intersection of North Zhejiang Road and Sixth Malu on the day before yesterday (6th). He was wearing a gray flannel suit, claimed to be named Ouyang, 28 years old, a local, a businessman, and opened room number 13. He lived alone in the hotel, appearing unhappy. Sand Barge "Xinshenglong" Encounters Pirates; Two Crew Members Killed, Two Kidnapped; Losses Approximately 5,000 Yuan 199

The "Xinshenglong" sand barge from Beikou was loaded with soybean oil, northern goods, etc. in Dalian and set sail for Shanghai. When sailing to the waters of Mount Dajishan, it suddenly encountered a large gang of pirates, driving two pirate ships, sailing at high speed against the wind. They opened fire and ordered them to stop. The "Xinshenglong" shipowner, surnamed Ye, seeing this, immediately instructed the helmsman to retreat. The two pirate ships chased after them, continuing to open fire, killing two crew members. At this point, the crew members were terrified and captured. The pirates, holding guns or knives and sticks, swarmed onto the ship, driving all the crew members into the bow of the ship. The pirates went to shipowner Ye's room, searched and looted more than seven hundred yuan in cash from the account box, and threw more than ten account books into the sea. Then, they searched the crew members, without exception. Among them, two crew members resisted the pirate search and were kidnapped by the pirates. Before leaving, the pirates, fearing that the ship would chase after them, smashed the ship's rudder, making it impossible to sail. The two pirate ships sailed east against the wind. The "Xinshenglong" ship's rudder was smashed by the pirates, resulting in a loss of sailing power. It drifted on the ocean surface for a day and night. Later, fortunately, a foreign warship passed by and saw it, and towed the "Xinshenglong" ship to Chongming to anchor. Yesterday, shipowner Ye took a boat from Chongming to Shanghai to report to the cargo owners and borrow silver dollars to purchase coffins for the two crew members who were killed by the pirates and to try to rescue the kidnapped crew members. It is said that the hull of the ship was also damaged in many places by the pirates' gunfire, and it can only be sailed after repairs. The amount stolen, including repair costs, is approximately 5,000 yuan.

Small Train in Chuansha Crushes Villager; Inspection 200

Xing Shen, a villager from Gaomiao Township, Pudong, 36 years old, carried a basket to the town to buy vegetables yesterday morning. He accidentally fell into the tracks of the Chuansha small train. He bent down to pick up the basket, but the train arrived and knocked him down, crushing him into two pieces, killing him instantly. The driver in the car immediately reported to the police station and ordered the local security officer to report to the local court. Prosecutor Tang, commissioned by the court, arrived at the scene to investigate and clarified that the relatives were instructed to collect the body for burial.

Old Collection of Rare Books for Sale 201

Wulin is a treasure trove of humanities, so rare thread-bound books are primarily from Hangzhou. During the Qianlong and Jiaqing periods, famous book collectors included Shousongtang, Xiaoshantang, Zhenqitang, and Zhibuzu Zhai. Their influence continued, and in the late Qing Dynasty, to modern times, collections such as Jiahuitang, Ding's, Fenghuatang, and Yang's were still rich. However, they have been separately entered into the Jiangnan Library, Peking University, and Tsinghua University. The only remaining large collection is the Jin family's Zhihuatang. Compared to the Ding and Yang families, it cannot be compared. However, the Jin family is a descendant of a prominent local family. Their ancestors held important positions in the capital during the Xianfeng and Tongzhi periods for decades. The collection of their ancestors and fathers was also not small, and among them were finely engraved famous annotated manuscripts that were difficult to find elsewhere. Jin's descendants, recently seeking food in all directions, worried that the collection would be scattered and lost, so they will sell it together with stone inscriptions. A detailed catalog has been compiled. The Jin family only wants to dispose of the collection, so the pricing is deliberately low, not competing with bookstores for profit. It is heard that many varieties are priced at only a few corners, not exceeding one yuan, so that poor scholars can also share the benefits and avoid the regret of missing out.

Hong Jinwen Commits Suicide by Hanging in Hotel 202

Hong Jinwen, from Zhenjiang, 26 years old, worked as a carpenter. At 10 pm the night before last, he went to the Rongxing Inn at No. 335 Xixinqiao Street in the French Concession, opened room number 3, and stayed overnight. For some unknown reason, he suddenly had a moment of despair and hanged himself on the bed frame. The next morning at 6 o'clock, the teaboy knocked on the door to empty the chamber pot, but there was no response. He pried the door open and found that Hong had already died. He immediately reported to the police station, which sent detectives to investigate. The body was transported to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for examination. As there were no relatives of the deceased, a report was made to Prosecutor Chen of the Second Special Court, who confirmed that the deceased had indeed died by hanging himself. The body was handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall for burial, pending identification by relatives.

Bandit Who Robbed Dancer's Gold Bracelet Sentenced; Sentenced to Three Years of Imprisonment 203

Tang Jinsheng, a recidivist bandit from Suzhou, 30 years old, robbed a pair of gold bracelets worth one hundred yuan worn by dancer Zhang Xiuying of Saint Anna, who was sitting in a rickshaw next to the Eight Immortals Bridge tram station in the French Concession at around 8 pm on the 3rd of this month, and fled. Detective Yin Baoke saw this, chased and caught him with the loot, and took him to the police station. It was found that the bandit had committed robbery and theft cases in the British Concession nine times. He was handed over to the First Special Court for prosecution, interrogation, and investigation of various circumstances, which have been reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the trial in the First Criminal Court, and sentenced Tang Jinsheng to three years of imprisonment for repeat robbery as a warning. The stolen items were returned to the owner to be taken away.

Reading and Answering Questions

On the Contradictions of Life (2) 214

Yesterday evening, we answered the first of the three questions raised by Mr. Li. Due to space constraints in this newspaper, we were unable to publish the full answer. Today, we will continue to publish the unfinished portion and further discuss the first part of the second question. Because the discussion for today and tomorrow will be more theoretical, please read carefully. The more we discuss this question, the easier it will become to understand. There are also brilliant examples for the readers' reference in life. - Editor

How do we explain the inherent contradiction of the life process itself? This means that a person's life cannot be separated from the social environment in which they live. They cannot be immune to the influence of the objective social existence. At the same time, they are a human being with flesh and blood and cannot be immune to the dictates of physiological laws. The contradiction of society, therefore, determines the contradiction of life. The contradictions of previous societies were not as great as those of modern society, so the reflection of contradictions in the lives of ancient people was also more moderate, and that was the reason. Under the feudal social system, because there were contradictions between landlords and serfs, naturally, two different conflicting thoughts would form in people's minds. Because feudal morality advocated asceticism, the opposition between morality and sexual desire would be presented in people's behavior. All of these become forms of conflict and are bound to be manifested as open and covert struggles in people's behavior. In the literature under the feudal system, we have seen many moving and tragic dramas of the conflict between love and morality, and customs. The lives of the protagonists in these stories sometimes reached extremes, and therefore, countless people committed suicide. Can we say that a young man or woman who commits adultery under asceticism is immoral? If we stand from a scientific standpoint to examine, we do not find it strange or immoral. We only feel that the contradiction presented in the lives of these "criminal" young men and women is "Should morality be maintained or should physiological needs be satisfied?" Can we call the contradictions in thought or action caused by this morbid or irregular?

Of course, from a legal point of view, it should be discussed separately.

Since human life is a reflection of objective social existence, the more contradictory and fragmented the society, especially in today's chaotic social changes, the more complex and contradictory human life becomes. This is not only manifested in thought, but also in action. All of this needs no explanation. As long as we look back at the lives of our ancestors eighty years ago and compare them with our current lives, we can suddenly understand.

The above answers the first theme raised by Mr. Li, explaining that the phenomenon of contradictions in life is determined by the inherent contradiction of the life process itself. It is not appropriate to discuss in detail the three aspects of contradictions in modern life.

(3) Why are there contradictions between thoughts?

As mentioned earlier, the phenomenon of contradictions in life is a manifestation of the conflicting contradictions of the life process. Life is a process, constantly changing and developing. The driving force that constitutes this change and development is naturally contradiction, but this contradiction is only a reflection of the social and natural development process. After the active role of human practice in social life, it becomes the fighting force that drives the flow of life.

So-called thought and action are inherently inseparable. Thought itself is originally a kind of action. To oppose thought and action is not a correct view. However, because thought is a latent action, unlike the concrete manifestation of action, it forms two different aspects in form. Because the process of shifting from latent action to concrete action is a rushing process, contradictions arise between the two. Furthermore, regarding the so-called contradictions between thoughts, it is only because thought is also a process, constantly changing, and what promotes the change of thought is the conflict between several different factors that are reflected in people's minds. The same principle applies to contradictions between actions. No need to elaborate. In short, in this section, we do not intend to completely separate these three aspects. The reason for separating the narratives is for the convenience of explanation. Readers should not misunderstand that they are unrelated to each other.

First, let's explain why thoughts present a contradictory phenomenon.

Since thought cannot stop at a certain stage, it must naturally develop. This includes: new thoughts and old thoughts cannot coexist and cannot but conflict, because this shift must be through practice. Social practice reflected in people's thinking is naturally colorful, but no matter how complex, intricate, diverse, and rich social practice is, what is reflected in people's thinking is not like taking a photo and taking it all in as it is. Because people's thinking itself has a dynamic effect, it has the dynamic effect of accepting a certain film and rejecting a certain film. This is due to his special living conditions. Special living conditions are the boundary markers that constitute the development of a person's thought. But this is not to say that thought has no way to go when it reaches this boundary marker, it can still develop, but it must first destroy this boundary marker. Naturally, when thought reaches the process of destroying the boundary marker, it must go through thousands of times of rushing and fighting. This road cannot be imagined as a smooth straight line, but is often winding. During this period, the storm of thought forms the contradictory phenomenon between thought and thought. Furthermore, in terms of the development of thought, thought is always a bit conservative, and external images are often not easily absorbed, and many fierce battles must also be gone through during this period. Even with regard to the thought process that is loyal to one's own special living environment, it is not that someone is born with the content of this thought. He must also go through a stage from unconsciously gradually entering consciousness. Contradictions of thought are bound to occur in this journey as well, forming a kind of contradictory phenomenon.

Generally speaking, the development process of thought is always progressive, but in today's society, it is not uncommon for the ruling thought to conquer the ruled thought and absorb the thought of other classes as its content. It can be said that thought can also develop downward, but this also has a certain limit, up to the point before one's own class becomes conscious. However, whether upward or downward, contradictions will appear in the process.

Therefore, it is extremely normal for thoughts to conflict and present contradictions. However, sometimes it takes an extremely subtle state, and sometimes it is clearly obvious. This is the order in which the thought process changes from gradual to sudden. If there is no gradual change, there will naturally be no sudden change. With gradual change, there cannot but be sudden change. For example, a person who is determined to commit suicide, his suicide is not decided overnight, his pessimistic thoughts have long existed before the suicide. Suicide is just a sudden change. Some people think it is very strange to see a person's betrayal, but in fact, this is a shallow view. Zheng Xiaoxu's willingness to be a traitor has its own process of being a traitor, it is not achieved in one night.

As for the small contradictions manifested in thought, they naturally occur every day. A linguist may often make jokes in his daily speech, and a logician may often say many illogical things. These are all contradictions, small waves in the process of rushing, and are not surprising.

Education News

Banners Flutter on Longhua Road: Student Army of This City Holds General Review Yesterday; Wu Tiecheng and Pan Youqiang Serve as General Review Officers; More Than 3,000 People Are Spirited and Neatly Dressed; Merchant Marine and Other Five Schools Have the Most Outstanding Drill Performance; Shooting This Morning and Flag Presentation and Awards This Afternoon 215

The military training students of various high schools and above in this city held the final general review of the 22nd year at Longhua Airport starting at 9:00 AM yesterday. 3,875 military training students from 35 schools and 38 military instructors actually arrived. Mayor Wu and Director Pan served as the general review officers, and the Panchen Lama also attended to observe. Yesterday, because the weather was suitable, the military students of various schools were spirited and the results were quite satisfactory. The details are recorded as follows:

丨Review Situation丨 Participating Teams 216

The military training students who participated in the review yesterday totaled 3,875 people from 25 schools and 38 military instructors. The order of their arrangement is as follows: 120 people from the Merchant Marine School, 287 from Jiaotong University, 91 from the Sino-French Institute of Technology, 160 from Tongji University, 115 from Jinan University, 120 from Daxia University, 139 from Guanghua University, 230 from Fudan University, 150 from Datong University, 112 from Dongya University, 135 from the School of Commerce, 85 from Zhengfeng, 80 from Hujiang University, 36 from the School of Law, 114 from Jingye, 108 from Xinlu, 110 from Fuzhong, 172 from Private Shangzhong, 110 from Fushi, 394 from Minli, 103 from Qingxin, 153 from the Chinese Vocational School, 150 from Guanghua Affiliated High School, 80 from Jianguo, 52 from Aurora Affiliated High School, 132 from Nanyang Model, 92 from Pudong, 90 from Jinan Affiliated High School, 61 from Nanyang Senior Business, 24 from Daxia Affiliated High School, 60 from Huiling, 38 from Junyi, 52 from Qingnian, 35 from Zhaohe, 41 from Mailun, and 26 from the Daxia Female Nursing Team.

A Glimpse of the Venue 217

Starting in front of the Longhua Road Garrison Command, slogans were posted along the way, and a colorful pine and cypress archway was erected with the horizontal inscription "I Wu Wei Yang" and the couplet "Reviewing the armed soldiers, hoping to strive for strength and eliminate the humiliation of the sick man," "Paying attention to youth military training makes them know that only then can they have the courage to promote the spirit of the nation." There was also an archway at the entrance of the review venue, with the couplet "Taking off the Confucian uniform and putting on military uniform, civility is not weak," "Wielding spears and protecting the country, I Wu Wei Yang." The review platform was set up at the west end of the venue, with a white cloth horizontal banner "Shanghai High School and Above Military Training Students Final General Review of the 22nd Year" suspended above it, and the couplet "Gathering all the healthy children of Shanghai to show the spirit of advocating martial arts and clearing the humiliation of the people," "Relying on years of military training to strengthen the physique and become the pillars of the country" hanging next to it. The flag of the Party and the State was suspended in the middle, and flowers and various prizes were displayed on the platform. The visitor seats and the rest areas for female students and military police were on the left and right sides of the platform. A temporary shed was set up on the left side of the venue for military students to rest. Along the road and around the venue, police officers and soldiers from the Gendarmerie Regiment were responsible for security. The Municipal Health Bureau specially dispatched an ambulance to the venue at all times. The Public Security Bureau band came to the venue to play music. Four large loudspeakers were set up in the venue, and the speeches could be clearly heard throughout the venue.

Guests in Attendance 218

In addition to the general review officers Wu Tiecheng and Pan Youqiang, those who attended included Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Jia Botao of the Security Office, Chen Ce of the Municipal Defense Council, Liu Yunfang of the Municipal Council, Gao Yunfeng of the Jiangsu National Military Training Council, Yao Yude of the Taxation Department, Xu Zeyu of the Municipal Education Association, Leng Xueqiao of the Boy Scouts Council, Han Juemin of the Greater Education Federation, and more than a hundred other guests. The Tibetan Living Buddha Panchen Lama and Commander Li Mo'an also attended to observe yesterday.

School Uniforms 219

The uniforms of the various schools were quite different. The colors included black, dark blue, green, gray, yellow, and white, with gray and yellow being more common. There were two types of hat styles: rimmed and stiff rimmed. However, Pudong Middle School wore pot-shaped copper hats. Most of the shoes worn were leather shoes and running shoes, only the Private Shangzhong and Pudong Middle School wore straw sandals. Except for a few students who were empty-handed, all schools had wooden guns, and the military appearance was very neat. The female nursing team of Daxia University wore white hats and long robes of Shilin cloth, with a red cross white cloth wrapped around their left arms, which was especially unique.

Review Begins 220

The review began at 9:00 AM. The chief commander was Chen Zhaoxin, the military instructor of Jiaotong University. He held a command knife and rode a white horse, first reporting the number of people in front of the platform, and then began the review. Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and other guests circled the venue for a military parade. Then, the military students of various schools marched in columns in front of the review platform in accordance with the order, with neat steps and bright flags, extremely mighty. Then, Mayor Wu, Director Pan, Director Pan, Director Wu, Li Zhaochen and others successively delivered training speeches. The morning review ended, and the guests were invited to lunch by the Garrison Command.

Training Results 221

At 1:30 PM, the inspection continued. The program consisted of squad instruction and platoon instruction. Schools were divided into four groups. All groups except the fourth group had nine schools each. Judges Zhang Jintang, Xie Weiyuan, Wei Guomo, Li Jiachu, Shen Yulin, Wei Jizhong, Gao Yunfeng, and Cai Xinya were assigned to each group to evaluate. According to the set movements, they conducted drills separately. The drills lasted for more than three hours. The judges determined that the best performing schools were Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Merchant Marine School, Fudan University, and Datong University. These five schools were gathered in front of the reviewing stand for further drills, which were personally evaluated by Chief Inspector Pan Youqiang.

In the end, the Wusong Merchant Marine Vocational School, under the instruction of instructor Tao Yishan, who issued clear commands and whose students demonstrated orderly steps, high spirits, and consistent formations, scored 87 points, winning first place. Second place went to Fudan Affiliated Middle School, third to Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, fourth to Fudan University, and fifth to Datong University. Subsequently, Director Pan told the Shanghai News Agency reporter that the performance of all schools was excellent this time, and these five schools had the best training results. The final ranking will be determined after averaging the scores from the parade and marching ceremony.

Smoke Bomb Performance 222

Finally, Fudan University demonstrated smoke bombs and Han Wu parachutes, with a total of nine participants. All wore white shirts, each carrying two smoke bombs. They were arranged in a line, placing the bombs about ten meters apart. Upon the instructor's command, each person lit the fuses. After about two seconds, white smoke billowed out, obscuring the sky and making it impossible to see across the way. After ten minutes, the smoke dissipated, and daylight returned. According to the school's instructor, the smoke bomb was invented by a chemistry professor at Fudan University and contained no toxic gas. The outer shell was made of iron. During the January 28th Incident, the school participated in the battle and used this bomb. Then, they demonstrated the Han Wu parachute, with four participants. Each person held a parachute containing gunpowder. Upon reaching the destination, a pile of grass, they placed the parachute down. After striking the handle a few times, the gunpowder exploded in a few minutes, and flames shot into the sky, bathing the entire field in red light. This parachute was designed to burn enemy granaries and was also invented by the school.

Today's Program 223

Starting at 8:00 AM today, a live ammunition shooting competition will be held at the shooting range at the West Fort of Gaochang Temple. Each school will send three participants. At 3:30 PM, a flag awarding ceremony will be held at Longhua Airport, and awards will be given. Each school can send a platoon of student soldiers to participate in the award ceremony.

|Excerpts from Speeches| Mayor Wu's Speech 224

Commander-in-chief, instructors, and students, in today's world, peace cannot be maintained internationally without armaments, and national independence and ethnic survival cannot be maintained without strength. China has faced extreme difficulties in the past, and is now facing multiple national crises, but China's future is bright. The reason China has been so difficult in the past and present is that it has lacked substantial armaments and strength for decades. The future of China lies in the youth of today. Today's youth are the masters of the future, but to be a master, one must have knowledge and ability to manage the country in the future. Therefore, the Kuomintang and the National Government must educate and train the youth of China today. In terms of academic education, we must equip the youth with modern knowledge so that they can continue to build the country in the future. In terms of military training, we must militarize all students so that they can hold weapons to defend the nation in the future. This kind of education and training is to strengthen the power of the people, so that they can shoulder the great responsibilities of the country and hold weapons to defend the nation in times of national crisis. Now we are preparing to strengthen human resources and national power, but students and youths must not forget the spirit of fearlessness that Sun Yat-sen told us, and the morals of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, responsibility, and order that Chiang Kai-shek told us. Chinese youth have been too scattered in the past. Military training can militarize them, and a strict organization can transform customs. I hope students will thoroughly implement this, and in the future, they will definitely become good and powerful citizens, and only then will they be qualified to be masters of China and build China's national rejuvenation.

Director Pan's Speech 225

Today, after watching your march, I feel very satisfied. The enemy is always laughing at us. Now, we can achieve this result with only two hours of military training each week. No other nation can do this, and no other country can achieve this result with only two hours of military training each week. This is very comforting. Shanghai is the center of China's economy and culture. Its position is very important. Students, you must know that Shanghai's material construction is built with the blood of the Chinese mainland flowing into Shanghai, which is why this modern Shanghai was built. In Shanghai, we are constantly subjected to enemy interference and oppression. Young students, we must not forget that many students spend their spare time going to dance halls, and consider it fashionable to wear Western suits and speak foreign languages. These are not the Chinese youths. Therefore, the meaning of military training is entirely the lifeline of the Chinese nation, and it is to teach people how to be citizens and how to survive. In the past, student movements have shed blood many times, and the lessons of the May 30th Massacre show that we have no military power. The Indian revolution has been going on for a long time without success, also because it lacks armed forces. Therefore, today, regardless of any nation, education is advancing on both fronts, and military training is so important that all countries are implementing a conscription system. Before China implements conscription, it is necessary to train the youth to defend the country in the future.

Director Pan's Speech 226

Today, seeing the achievements of the students, I am very excited. The purpose of military training is to have the power to defend oneself and the country. To defend oneself and the country, one must have the spirit to hold weapons to defend the nation. In military training, it is especially hoped that everyone will pay attention to unity. One must have a spirit of sincere unity. If one only receives military skills training and neglects the spirit of unity, it is like having only the skin and neglecting the spirit. In the end, one will still not be able to defend oneself and the country. In the past, many Chinese armies could not save the country, and this was the reason. Now we are paying attention to student military training, which means incorporating soldiers into learning, building the foundation of a new army in schools, and only with a spirit of unique love and unity can we make up for the shortcomings of the past and achieve our desired goals.

Director Wu's Speech 227

Today, inspecting the military training of Shanghai's high schools and above, we should have a profound feeling, that is, since the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, the people of the whole country have known the danger of the country and the nation. Therefore, in this period of severe national crisis, everyone knows the weakness of self-defense capabilities, which has caused the enemy to attack repeatedly. We must avenge our humiliation, defend the country, and revive

the nation. First, we must strengthen our strength, especially by building that strength on the youth. The youth are the soldiers standing at the forefront. The country has reached a very critical point, and they must be the vanguard. At the same time, the world crisis is imminent. A major war in 1936 is about to break out. China must strive forward in these two or three years to cope with this major war. This depends entirely on the youth of the whole country redoubling their efforts to strengthen their strength, and only then can they save the country and the nation.

Director He's Speech 228

Director He's reply briefly stated that today is the first day of the inspection of military training students in Shanghai. He received many speeches from the Chief Inspector and guests, and will accept them and follow their instructions to work hard on national military training. However, he himself is deeply concerned that he does not have enough sincerity to move towards the great goal of national military training and shoulder the great task of national rejuvenation.

The Great Education Federation Yesterday Issued a "Declaration to Maintain the Dignity of Professors": Academic Morality Is the Foundation of Professors; Enticing and Confusing Youth Is Not Tolerated by National Law 229

The Federation of University Faculty and Staff in this city previously submitted a proposal on how to maintain the dignity of professors at its tenth joint meeting of executive and supervisory committees, which was referred to the Standing Committee for review. It is now known that the proposal has been resolved by the fourth meeting of the Standing Committee and will be issued as a declaration. The full text of the declaration is excerpted below: Since its inception, this Federation has advocated the two major propositions of cultural revival and academic salvation as the fundamental plans for survival. Over the years, colleagues have sharpened their minds day and night, based on this meaning, to encourage each other, and have worried and pondered day and night, also based on this meaning, to call on comrades. Since the establishment of this Federation until now, a year has passed in a flash. Although restricted by financial, temporal, and human resources, the aspirations and accomplishments have failed to reach even one in ten thousand. However, within the meager reach of colleagues, we have always tried our best to create

An Academic Environment 230

to stimulate profound interest, to cultivate integrity and conduct, to preserve the national essence, and to transform declining customs, in order to create a trend that can create public opinion and moral force, and win social sympathy. This is what colleagues often take comfort in, and it is also enough to plead not guilty to the people of the country. Establishing a country and cultivating people is a century-old plan, which lies in education. The way of education lies not only in imparting knowledge, but also in the influence of personality. Today's youth in schools are the masters of China in the future. The relationship between professors and students is no different from that between parents and children. As a teacher, one must act as a model for others, and one's words must be a law for others. Its influence on the country and society is extremely important. Therefore, university professors should

Cultivate Morality 231

enrich knowledge, rectify oneself and lead by example, shape and cultivate, and silently transform and influence. Only then can they fulfill the great responsibilities of imparting the Tao, teaching, and resolving doubts, and fulfill the natural responsibility of becoming a model of virtue and talent. These are the golden rules that colleagues always uphold without losing, and they are also the guidelines that the entire academic community should practice. However, based on the observations of colleagues over the years, this meaning has not yet been understood by the entire academic community. At a time when the Ministry of Education has repeatedly issued orders to rectify the academic style of the country and the government is exhausted to promote propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, there are still some individuals who are suspicious of virtuous talents, hindering meritorious deeds, issuing orders from above, twisting and rising to the hall, engaging in horizontal and vertical intrigue, hooking and fighting, tilting and squeezing, inciting discord, plotting secret calculations, slanderously injuring, excluding dissidents, pursuing selfishness and plundering, and seeking to vent personal grievances, causing scholars to be in danger and people to be wary. Pure youth become accustomed to fraud and schemes, and the sacred altar becomes like a

Political Battleground 232

sacrificing students' wealth, damaging the country's vitality, and destroying the inherent morality of the nation. The negative impact it gives to students and the hidden dangers it plants in society are truly unimaginable. Colleagues witness this with fear and worry about it. We have thought deeply and carefully that the best way to save the situation is to restore the ancient style of respecting teachers and valuing the Tao. The thorough method is to return to the sincere cooperation of the principal, professors, and students. There must be teachers who teach tirelessly before there can be students who never tire of learning. There must be a principal who treats scholars with courtesy and is happy to do good before there can be professors who maintain their integrity and devote themselves to academics. Professors must take

Academic Morality 233

as the foundation and should be kind, respectful, and dignified towards students, respecting each other with morality. They cannot be induced by power and should not degrade their personality, giving young people a bad impression. Students must respect teachers and value the Tao, and they must be able to distinguish right from wrong. They must not blindly follow and echo, allowing themselves to be driven and striving to become talents for society and pillars of the country. The principal must be humble, know how to use people well, love goodness and forget power, and should not regard the school as a government office, treating professors as subordinates. If these three parties work together, the school will have a harmonious atmosphere, and teachers and students will be as close as children and siblings. Only then can the entire success of education be achieved and the great task of revival be shouldered together. From now on, if anyone dares to have ulterior motives,

Entice and Confuse Youth 234

to plot wrongdoing and manipulate the school, they will be pests in the cultural world and will not be tolerated by national cleansing discipline. Those who cherish themselves will be ashamed to associate with them, and colleagues should rise up to attack them, expel them from the academic community, and abandon them with the people of the country. As the ancients said, the more a gentleman yields, the more presumptuous a villain becomes. If the Tao is one foot high, the devil is ten feet high. Colleagues only rely on personality and righteousness to fight the devil. This declaration is hereby made.

Education Fees for April and May in This City Will Be Issued Within the Month; Teachers and Staff of Municipal Primary Schools Pledged Yesterday; Secretary-General Yu and Director Pan of the Education Bureau Gave Satisfactory Replies 237

Since the Shanghai War, the financial revenue of this city has suddenly decreased sharply. Therefore, the various expenses of the municipal government have had to be greatly tightened. However, the educational expenses of the city have always been maintained in order to ensure that the municipal schools are not affected by the war. At times, the municipal treasury is tight, and there may be some delays, but Mayor Wu and Directors Pan (Education) and Cai (Finance) will definitely find ways to issue them as soon as possible. Previously, teachers of primary and secondary schools in this city petitioned the municipal government and the Education Bureau due to overdue education fees. Mayor Wu was responsible for planning and explained the financial difficulties of the municipal government to the teachers, and the matter came to an end. Recently, the municipal treasury has become extremely tight again, resulting in the delayed payment of the expenses of municipal primary schools. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, eighty-six representatives from the primary school teachers of the city petitioned the Education Bureau and the Municipal Government. Director Pan of the Education Bureau was out on official business. He informed them by telephone of the efforts to raise funds and said that he had contacted the Municipal Government and the Finance Bureau. The expenses for April will be issued in mid-month, and the expenses for May will be issued in the next ten days. It is hoped that the expenses for June can be issued before the summer vacation. After the principal of Xicheng Primary School informed the representatives, the representatives went to the Municipal Government to petition. Secretary-General Yu Hongjun met with them. The representatives immediately stated the reasons for the petition. Yu expressed sympathy and promised to instruct the Finance Bureau to do its best to raise funds in order to issue them as soon as possible, and told the representatives to work with peace of mind. The representatives returned satisfied.

The 686th meeting of the Zhejiang Provincial Government resolved that students of provincial normal schools will be subsidized half their meals by the province starting from the 23rd academic year. After graduation, they must serve in elementary schools for more than one year. It has now been included in the education budget and has been passed to order the schools to comply.

The French Government Asks the Parliament to Pass a Motion to Participate in the Olympics; Submits a Draft Law to Allow Participation; Stipulates That 240 Athletes Will Be Sent 249

(Havas Agency, Paris, 7th) The government has recently submitted a draft law to the Chamber of Deputies, requesting permission for French athletes to participate in the 1936 Olympic Games in Berlin. The draft law states that the Olympic Games were originally a legacy of ancient Greece, and were revived thanks to the enthusiasm for sports of Baron Coubertin of France. Therefore, France must send representatives to participate. The bill also stipulates that France should send 140 athletes to participate in the games, and another 40 to participate in various winter sports.

Dispute of the Hunan Basketball Association 262

According to a letter from the Qunyi Basketball Team, "To Whom It May Concern: Having read the newspaper report, we have learned that the Hunan Basketball Competition organized by the Liuxing Sports Association has falsely accused our team members of assaulting the inspector, Mr. Wu Zibin, and has therefore cancelled the qualifications of all of our team's A and B groups. According to the competition on that day, although Mr. Wu's refereeing was repeatedly negligent, our team members have always adhered to the rules and morals without any impolite behavior. Therefore, our team has four reasons for protest (the protest letter has been submitted to the association). The people who clashed with Mr. Wu that day were all spectators who were caused by unfair emotion. Shen Bao Radio Weekly

Pick-up Revival Method 265

— Ming Xiang

The pick-up (commonly known as a record player cartridge) is an indispensable accessory for high-end radios. After being used for a while, its effectiveness often gradually decreases, and the sound becomes weak. The main cause is the U-shaped permanent magnet inside. Although there is an armature between the two poles of this magnet, the magnetic force lines are not interrupted, but the armature must leave a considerable gap with the magnet in order to move, so the magnetic circuit can never be completely sealed. The magnetic force is often lost, and after a long time, it gradually disappears completely and becomes ineffective. The method of revival is simply to reapply a strong permanent magnetic field.

The first step is to identify the polarity of the pick-up magnet. The method is very simple, you can test it with a magnetic needle. The point indicated by the north pole of the magnetic needle is the south pole of the pick-up. Then prepare another horseshoe-shaped permanent magnet, which must have very reliable magnetism. The size should be selected to match the pick-up, and place it flat on the pick-up. When placing it, be sure to pay attention to the polarity of both ends of the horseshoe magnet, which must be opposite to that of the pick-up, to be effective. Otherwise, it cannot be revived. The position of the horseshoe magnet should be such that its two ends are close to the bottom of the pick-up. Then tighten it so that it does not move (as shown in the picture).

Place the record on the turntable, turn on the radio's amplifier, and then place the pick-up mentioned above on it, or you will be surprised. This suddenly loud tone is sometimes more beautiful and pleasant than a new pick-up.

Finally, there is one more point to remedy. Because the newly added horseshoe magnet increases the weight of the pick-up, it strengthens the pressure on the record. The rotation of the record will be hindered, even stopped. The remedy is to add an appropriate weight to the other end of the pick-up handle to balance it. This way, the pressure of the pick-up needle can be adjusted to the appropriate degree.

Matching Method of Common Antenna 266

— Yi Zhi

Using one antenna for several radios to receive signals was once considered impossible. This is because adjusting one machine will affect the reception of other radios, causing the signal to change and cause interference. However, if this antenna is connected in series with a set of separate coils and capacitors, changing the total impedance (Impededance) from each radio to the antenna, in other words, even if the total impedance from each radio to the antenna is different, it is as if there are several antennas. Then, whether one, two, three, or four machines use this common antenna, it will not affect the reception. It is the same as each machine using its own antenna.

The matching method is shown in Figure 1. This common antenna can be used for four radios. L1 is 20 turns, L2 is 30 turns, L3 is 40 turns, L4 is 50 turns. Use 28-gauge enameled wire to wind around a bakelite tube with a diameter of 2 inches. C is a 0.0001 farad fixed capacitor. After the coils and capacitors are grouped and matched according to Figure 1, they are placed in a shielding cover and led out to the lead-in wires of each radio (as shown in Figure 2) for application.

Wireless Radio Treasure Finder 267

— Li Yuanqing

There is a story in "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio" that says: "There was a man named Feng who released a giant turtle with a white spot on its forehead. Later, the giant turtle repaid his great kindness and gave him a little man only an inch long. Since Feng wore this turtle treasure, he could see all the gold and silver treasures hidden under the Yellow Springs. Later, he dug up hundreds of thousands of coins in his bedroom, and countless wide objects in various places. Feng became as rich as a prince because of this." This is, of course, a story fabricated by a novelist, and no one dares to believe that there is such a fact. However, the treasure finder introduced in this article can truly assume the task of the turtle treasure and indicate the location of the treasure for you. When an old-fashioned regenerative radio without an isolation device is in use, if our hands approach any part of the radio, a kind of crazy screech will often be caused in the speaker. This is because the radio is sensing the human body. The basic principle of the treasure finder described below is designed based on this special phenomenon.

The first picture shows the appearance of the finder. A is the transmitter, (Transmitter) its internal structure is shown in the second picture, L is a loop coil wound around the outside of the wooden box, a total of ten turns, with a center tap drawn out at the fifth turn. B is the receiver. (Receiver) Its internal structure is shown in the third picture. The loop coil L is also wound ten times.

When using, first adjust the receiver to resonate with the transmitter. Then vibrate the wooden box of the transmitter to the extent that no sound is heard in the receiver. At this time, the coils L must form a right angle with L. Usually, the surrounding radio waves are scattered in a regular pattern (as shown in the upper part of the fourth picture), but once they encounter metals such as gold and silver, a part of the radio waves will be absorbed and distorted. Since the emitted radio waves are unbalanced (Balance), the earphone will get audio signals.

In order to further improve the sensitivity of the receiver, R can be adjusted or a regenerative coil can be installed in the detection tube (as shown by the lines in the third picture) to generate oscillation. In this way, what is usually heard in the earphone is only the frequency difference between the transmitter and the receiver (Beat Frequency), a kind of hissing screech. When the finder encounters metal, the frequency of the transmitter or receiver itself will be affected, and as a result, the tone generated in the earphone will change.

The materials required for the finder and their values are as follows:

(1) Transmitter part

One wooden box (dimensions are shown in Figure 1A) C (variable capacitor) ·0.00025 µfd Cl (fixed capacitor) ·0.00025 µfd ·lC3 l·5µf·Rl l5 ohms R lI l megohm·

(2) Receiver part

One wooden box (dimensions are shown in Figure 1B) CC1 l·0.00025mf·Variable capacitor, C2 l·0.00025mt·lC3 l·0.00025mf·lC4, C5mf, fixed capacitors R1 l2 l me gohm, R2 l22/Iohm; fixed resistor R3 l0·I00000·0hm variable resistor.

Small Experience Volume 268

— Wu Shanzhang

Installed a radio for someone else, and the volume was not very satisfactory after testing. Therefore, I suspected that the antenna was too short, or the primary coil was too small, so I added a coil (about forty or fifty turns) to the antenna post. Although the volume increased, the selectivity was not good. When I moved it to the ground wire post, the result was the same. Finally, I added a coil to each of the ground and antenna connecting posts, making the two coils parallel. The selectivity was also not good. I then made the two coils perpendicular, and I was satisfied. The volume increased, and there was no problem with the selectivity.

Materials for Making Fixed Capacitors Yourself

To make fixed capacitors yourself, everyone always uses cigarette tin foil because it is easy to get and available everywhere. But in recent years, cigarette tin foil has been made of extremely thin aluminum, which is very brittle. If it is not done well, it is very easy to break, and it is necessary to redo it, which is very uneconomical in terms of time. Therefore, I found other easy-to-get materials to replace it, then the empty toothpaste tube is the best. It is thick and soft, and very easy to handle. Furthermore, the insulation of the fixed capacitor can be made of soft photographic film. The gelatin on the surface is washed away to form a transparent artificial ivory (Celluloid) thin sheet to replace the mica sheet. The results are also good. It can be used as a bypass capacitor and a grid capacitor. Soft film is not easy to get, so use waxed paper, but the insulation is inferior.

Shielding Cover

Mr. Li Yuanqing has already introduced the shielding cover in this magazine. This is just using waste. Wash a metal can clean and you can use it. Choose one with a suitable height and diameter to use as a shielding cover between vacuum tubes or coils, which is very convenient.

Single-Tube Machine with Excellent Sensitivity 269

— Liu Tongkang

Out of a moment of interest, I will now write down the results of the experiment during this year's spring vacation, which are more satisfactory, here for the reference of those who like it.

Because I often see circuits for single-tube radios made with a No. 33 output power tube published in this magazine and other magazines and newspapers, it is said that the performance is superior to ordinary two-tube machines, so I became interested and tested it. The results were not bad, but the only shortcomings were unstable oscillation and uneconomical power consumption. After a short period of improvement, I gradually became satisfied. Figure 1 shows the circuit of this machine. The No. 33 vacuum tube in the original machine has been replaced with a No. 38 automotive tube here, and the performance is exactly the same as that of No. 33. Because it has one more cathode, it can be used for both AC and DC, especially when using AC power, the AC noise can be as quiet as using DC. The filament voltage is 6.3 volts and the filament current is not very large, similar to No. 33. This machine adopts electronic coupling regeneration, so the oscillation is very stable, and the noise is also the smallest. This is something that the original circuit cannot match. In short, this machine is excellent in selectivity, volume, and sound quality.

In the figure, coil 1 is wound with 32-gauge enameled wire in ten turns on a diameter paper or plastic tube as L, at a distance of two cents, and the same wire is wound in one hundred and twenty-five turns as L1. After winding, there is no need to cut the wire head. Draw one end and wind thirty turns in the opposite direction as L2. C is a variable capacitor for adjusting the wavelength. The capacity is 0.00035 MFD. C1 is a grid capacitor with 0.0001 MFD. C2 is a bypass capacitor with 1 MFD, which is used to avoid noise when rotating R1. C3 is a fixed capacitor with 0.002 MFD. C4 is a fixed capacitor with 0.006 MFD. R is a grid leak with 5 megohms. R1 is a 50,000-ohm potentiometer for controlling regeneration. The RFC high-frequency choke coil in the figure is closely related to the radio, so it is advisable to use a high-quality one. A electricity can be used in four series round batteries or changed from electric bell grid, B electricity is best to use one hundred and thirty-five volts or ninety volts that can be used up to one hundred and eighty volts, then the volume is even more grand, dry battery. This machine can play a small horn speaker for the entertainment of one room.

Records of Fragrant Imperial Incense 272

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing, Translated by Qin Shouou

The Chinese have a peculiar understanding of the sheng (mouth organ). Everyone considers the sheng as something that promotes lung disease. Some even say that if you split open a sheng that has been used for a slightly long time, you can often find blood inside. Although I have not witnessed this myself, there was indeed a eunuch in the palace who developed a severe cough because he blew the sheng too strenuously.

(The following are the pipa, guqin, trumpet, tang gong, flute, xiao, nao, and cymbals, etc. Translator's note: Most people probably know these musical instruments. The author's original text was specifically for Westerners, so it was described in great detail; therefore, there is no need to translate them directly here, so everything is omitted.)

The Empress Dowager's musicians all have assistants, as mentioned above. However, these assistants' musical knowledge is really not inferior to their main players. Because when performing music, the instruments used by their main players often need to be changed, and they are changed very quickly, often without informing their assistants what instrument to use. These assistants are entirely responsible for distinguishing and handing them the instruments that should be used. This, of course, cannot be handled by an amateur. Moreover, they must not only pass on the musical instrument that should be used but also hang the unused instruments on that large rack. The procedure is extremely troublesome!

Overall, the sound of the music played by the Empress Dowager's orchestra can truly be said to be very mysterious. When these musicians are playing, everyone wears a straight face, without any expression, like wooden puppets with mechanisms. I think that no matter how they play, they themselves have absolutely no feeling.

But in the Empress Dowager's eyes, apart from them, she could not find such great musicians in the world. (53)

Bitter Rice 274

— Hu Shu

I haven't eaten for several days, but I don't feel hungry. This may be the only ability of a patient. Although the muscles are thinning away like melting ice, the cost of food is saved after all. For people who work one day and eat the next, if they get sick and still have to eat, that would be the end of Ada's life. Not seeing a doctor, not taking medicine, lying in bed, tossing and groaning is already enough suffering. If the stomach is not good, the poor will have to die.

Although Ada is a worker, because he is alone and has no burden of a wife or children, his situation is usually not too bad. He eats three large bowls of rice for each meal, a large ball of ci fan (sticky rice) in the morning, and can smoke a few Gold Mouse brand cigarettes every day. He often eats and drinks baijiu (white liquor) and peanuts until he is drunk. When he is free, he makes a pot of strong tea and tells jokes and talks about news with a few like-minded friends, not knowing what is sorrow or what is hate. He works during the carefree daytime and sleeps at night. No one will bother him, and he will not bother anyone. Except for humming a few tuneless songs when his alcohol gets to him, he always greets people with a smile and is very friendly.

Citizen in National Crisis

However, since he suddenly contracted this illness, he has suffered a major blow to his spirit, and he has begun to feel sorry for the misery of his life and the cruelty of his encounter. Although he勉强 escaped from the hands of death, his once lively body has now become like a weak and frail woman. The smile on his face has long disappeared, and the wrinkles on his forehead are even denser and deeper.

"Damn it, I'm not very old, but I'm so delicate like this." This was the sigh he heard when he staggered and fell on the bed after returning from work after his illness.

Of course, Ada, who is about fifty years old, is not considered old, and he has no worries about finding food with his strength! He thought that he was born with a bitter life, and it was enough to have a mouthful of bitter rice. As long as he was willing to endure hardship, he would not worry about not having food. But he never thought that he would be troubled by not being able to eat now!

But pitifully, he still said: "Fortunately, my appetite has decreased now, otherwise, I would either die of hardship or starve to death!"
