Small Recipes

Method of Preserving Plums 277

— Qing Qu

The Book says, "If you make a soup, you only need salt and plums." Plums were known as something edible in ancient times. However, there is no explanation in the records on how to eat them. Even in other books such as "Qunfang Pu," "Nongzheng Quanshu," as well as "Ben Cao Gang Mu," and "Gujin Tushujicheng," there are records, and they can also treat diseases and serve as essential medicinal products. However, they are not very detailed. If someone could revise them and refer to the current scientific methods of preparation, I dare say that the benefits of plums would definitely be great. Therefore, I like to eat plums the most. Now, I will briefly write down several simple methods of preserving plums as follows.

Sugar-preserved: Take early, firm, green plums, and use a needle to prick them all around. Then soak them in a diluted solution of salt water (about four taels of salt and more than nine catties of water). After four hours, take them out, and then pour them into clear water to rinse them until the salty taste is completely removed. If you take ten catties of plums, then use six taels of cooked shellfish ash and soak them in clear water for up to twelve hours. Then remove the ash and make a sweet solution with about one catty of water and one catty of sugar. Pour the plums in, and add sugar once every two days (about a quarter of the first time) until the sweetness and plums are just right. In less than two weeks, the texture of the plum pulp will change, and when you eat it, you will only feel the sweetness and not the sourness, which is pleasant to the taste. If you often soak them in this sugary solution in the container, even after four or five years, they will not change their nature and spoil. If you don't like the color of the plums, you can also use copper sulfate or blue stone (the most convenient is to use the smallest chicken-eye coins used for making money) in the sugary solution (about two or three fen per ten catties of plums). However, do not overdo it, otherwise, it will contain excessive toxicity, not only emitting a very foul odor but also harmful to eat. If you can use the right amount, this method is very palatable, and the texture is firm and crisp, with a sound when chewed, no different from fresh plums. In the past, someone titled this kind of sugar preparation and called it "wind and rain plums," that's what it means!

Salt-preserved: Take green, hard, and firm plums, about two taels of salt per catty, and put them together in a ceramic container, and add hot water to prevent them from drying out. It is best to press heavy objects on top to prevent mold and other harms, and the salty taste is also easy to penetrate completely. If they are stored in a container, tightly covered to prevent air from entering, they can last a long time. If they are then dried in the sun, so that the bottom and top surfaces are all exposed to intense heat, after two or three weeks, the surface of the plums will develop a kind of salt frost, its color is pure white, and it is extremely beautiful. However, you must prevent rainwater from entering during drying. If you are not careful, it is most prone to mildew. This method was called "plum embryos" by the ancients and can be stored for more than ten years without spoiling. Because it always carries very fine salt particles, it looks quite like frost on the roof tiles, so it is also called "frost plums." If you make osmanthus and rose jam, and add the juice of these plums to it, the color of the osmanthus and roses will be even more yellow and red! Because its acidity is most capable of illuminating its pigment!

Medicine-preserved: Pour the plum embryos into clear water and soak them (for about ten hours) until the salt is completely removed. Then filter the water completely, and then mix them in a 50% sugar solution. It is necessary to remove the inherent sour taste of the plums. Even if the previous sugar solution is discarded, it is not a pity. Then add an extremely thick sugar solution to allow the plum pulp to seep into the sweetness until it is fully flavored. Mix with lemon slices, and mash it into a sauce. Then add cloves, mint, star anise, or extremely fragrant spices to add its qualities. Finally, add aged dried tangerine peel powder to it and expose it to the sun. At this time, it has become a sauce, and the volume of the plums has also floated and swollen. When it is slightly dry, it can be wrapped in wax paper. It can be eaten for a long time, and it is not only a refreshment during the journey, but also a medicine, because it is made with several medicinal flavors. Therefore, the words "Chen Pi Mei" (dried tangerine peel plums) sold on the market are the most famous, and this method is used!

Other preparation methods such as "plum paste" can be sweet or salty, depending on personal taste, and the color can also be green, yellow, red, or black. Its texture can be made into "paste," "glue," "juice," or "dew," depending on the preparation method. In the south, plum sauce is the main product, and in the north, sour plum soup is famous. Plum "juice," plum "jelly," and plum "smooth paste" are not ordinary preparation methods. Now, what is most well-known in the market is "Qing Yan Mei Zi" (clear salted plums) from Zhang Xiangfeng in Xiaonanmen, Shanghai. In addition, "Mei Pi" (plum skin) from Qingpu Zhujie Pavilion is also very famous. However, the sugar content of plum skin seems to be too heavy, and it loses the original nature of the plum. Is this perhaps evidence that most people who eat plums are afraid of sourness and like sweetness?

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 278

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 30: Watching the Bereaved Geese Off, Burying Heads to Defend the Territory, Bullet Piercing a Strong Arm, Blood Staining a Lonely City

Outside the house, only the sound of running footsteps could be heard, some running past, and some running back. This was precisely adding to the infinite amusement of the people in the plane. Seeing the people below from above was like ants on a hot stone, running around in confusion. He fixed his eyes on the place where people were running very densely, and with another轟 sound, he awarded a bomb. When this bomb landed, there was not only the sound that shattered people's eardrums, but also the flying sand turned into smoke and fog, rising several feet high. In that smoke and fog, a hand, a leg, and a section of body cavity of the common people flew. In short, what the people here had never dreamed of was seeing it with their own eyes. Although the soldiers and civilians in the fortress were very calm and did not think that this was a matter of life and death, this was the first time that the plane had visited, and the common people were running around and screaming like that, and everyone's hearts could not help but jump up. A batch of Pinghu goods were made in secret trading in the previous two days, and the price was heard to be 3.9 yuan, according to the rules of the foreign firm.

The Cocoon Market in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is Coming to an End

Zhejiang is about to end... Jiangsu's goods are booming

(Shaoxing Cocoon Bank stopped weighing) Shaoxing's new cocoons were listed earlier. The cocoon production in the four villages is eight years old. The improved cocoon averages only 24-25 yuan, and the native cocoon is 16-17 yuan. The silk farmers are losing money.

(Wuxian silkworm eggs are sold publicly) Jiangsu's spring cocoons are on the market for the first time, and farmers are accustomed to pre-ordering the next year's silkworm eggs after the spring cocoons are sold. The Wuxian Silkworm Improvement Zone is preparing for the public sale of silkworm eggs in accordance with the Silkworm Egg Control Measures promulgated by the construction. The east and west sides of Dongting Lake will be designated as cocoon bank control areas, and special public sale offices will be set up in Hukou Female Silkworm School, Provincial Su Agricultural School, etc. The measures will be formulated and implemented immediately.

K> Free Talk

We Need Museums 298

— Walter

Many things are self-evident in the West, but in our country require much explanation. For example, the need to drink water when thirsty is unquestionable for Westerners, but in our country, many disagree: some people fundamentally oppose drinking water or tea, advocating only eating a preserved plum or olive. Smoking a cigarette is no big deal daily; however, in the interior, it is forbidden, and soldiers seize them on the road.

But now, let us raise our voices again: We need museums!

The reason? There is no reason, we unconditionally need to build large museums.

Predictably, many will object: "The 'Manchukuo' has already been established in the Northeast, and people's livelihoods are so precarious. Are you heartless people going to waste the nation's money building useless museums? Our Dr. Zhang Jingsheng said it well: Selling Chinese antiques to foreign countries is very appropriate, because the money can be used to buy guns and cannons, which can be used to fight foreigners, and after defeating the foreigners, we can take them back. Like the precious jade of Chu, one does not need to return the lamb; it only adds age. Moreover, people barely have enough to eat, and you still want them to learn sculpting and oil painting? Clearly, you are slaves to a lost country. Even after the country is lost, you will still paint oil paintings? Still build museums?"

Another argument: "This is fundamentally a pastime for the bourgeoisie after eating Western food and smoking cigars. These bourgeois-smelling wastes, oil paintings! Sculptures! We inevitably and fundamentally despise them, so they are doomed to decline and inevitably will. We stand at the forefront of the world's cultural struggle and dare to say we don't want art, let alone the tiny, insignificant museums attached to it."

Another argument: "If the country really has some spare money, it might as well build several large Peking opera theaters or a few cinemas. This can both enlighten the people and increase revenue. Who wants to see some broken, dilapidated antiques coldly placed in a temple-like building? Therefore, I strongly advocate building theaters."

However, we need museums. The reason? There is no such reason.

By the Duillier River 299

— Old White

Qi Jun was one of my closest friends five years ago. Meeting again in this cold city this year, we both felt immense joy. Although we were good friends, closer than any other, we each had our own thoughts, which were vastly different. Often, late at night or during our conversations, I felt that this was a regrettable aspect of our friendship. I remember Qi Jun often telling me five years ago, "A person's thoughts can never be captured. You and I are like this because I believe in my thoughts; I think my thoughts are meaningful. No matter how worthless or boring my thoughts are considered by others, I must persevere."

Something always separated us: thoughts.

Qi Jun was a master of wasting himself. His view of life was one of enjoyment. He once said, "People live in the world to seek happiness; I live in the world to enjoy happiness and well-being every day. I will not worry about anything..." But what did I think after hearing his words? Could I correct and turn his incorrect thoughts around? I sometimes used stimulating words to advise him, but he was never moved. He thought his wasteful life was a joyous and meaningful expression. He said he needed waste, he needed happiness to regulate his life. He even said he would always embrace hedonism; even when he died, he would still be enjoying himself.

We parted in Naples. Qi Jun, filled with joy, stood on the deck of the ship and said to me, "Bai, you should go back now! I will definitely write to you after I arrive in Cairo..." Qi Jun's words deeply stung me, and I couldn't help but shed tears! But my tears were not for my attachment to Qi Jun; I was lamenting for Qi Jun, lamenting Qi Jun's youth, and even more so for many people like Qi Jun who waste their youth.

Qi Jun went to Cairo this time for no particular reason. He was going to play; to waste his precious youth in enjoyment. Since Qi Jun left me, his image has often been in my mind. Every night, I would think of him, and I would also think of many wasters.

This year, we met again in this place.

Qi Jun came to me almost every day, but his idea of enjoyment had not changed in the slightest.

In this lonely city, especially since I lived alone in this small house, and the landlady was not very talkative, I needed friends to come; because their presence could alleviate some of my melancholy.

Students and people working in factories came to me. They usually came at night, even in the deeper, quieter hours. So, during the day, I couldn't avoid loneliness, even though I was still studying at school. Now it was good; Qi Jun had finally reappeared in this place. The loneliness I felt during the day was gone.

Because it was spring, the air outside was very fresh. Qi Jun dragged me to the Duillier River for a leisurely stroll. The river water rippled with silver waves, reflecting the deep green coconut trees, almost turning into a beautiful picture. We sat under this coconut tree and talked about what had happened since we parted.

"Qi, you should have changed your thinking by now?" I said, patting Qi Jun's shoulder, but he did not answer me. He smiled and shook his head, indicating that his thinking had not changed.

"So... your thinking will never change?"

"Hmm..." Qi Jun said suddenly, as if remembering something. "Didn't you say that a person's thinking will never change?"

"Yes..." I said frankly. "Although that's true, I think your thinking, your decadent thinking, should change; you need to know that only a just and truthful thought is worthy of cherishing! Qi, are your thoughts just and truthful?"

Qi Jun did not speak; he was still smiling. A strange feeling occupied my heart. I thought of Qi Jun's youth, and I also thought of the youth of many wasters like Qi Jun. I was at a loss, and an immense sadness occupied me.

Suddenly, Qi Jun stood up. He yawned and began to walk back and forth on the grass. Qi Jun's shiny leather shoes rubbed against the grass, making a proud, strange sound. I dared not look at Qi Jun's face, because if I saw his face, I would think of a person's life, of a person's youth. Although Qi Jun had not worried or grieved in recent years, a few deep wrinkles had been drawn on his forehead. I felt that it was a pity for a person to grow old slowly in enjoyment and waste; why doesn't a person do what he should do? Why does a young person waste his youth in enjoyment? ...The flames of depression were burning in my heart. I stared blankly at Qi Jun's pair of shoes, brighter than mirrors, beneath the long flannel trousers, walking back and forth on the grass... It was like I was having a dream, a painful dream.

Flowers That Don't Bloom 300

— Yingzi

The person who plants flowers that don't bloom is lonely.

However, the expectation of flowers blooming is more meaningful than looking at a tree full of blossoms. Rather than watching flowers bloom and fall, it's better not to have flowers bloom at all. I love the graceful, lonely, empty courtyard and the flowers and trees that don't bloom.

Planting a few flowers occasionally is just learning to plant. There is no pretense of elegance, and there is not even a desire to see a flower bloom. Moreover, I truly feel an infinite emptiness about this – in terms of knowledge and experience in horticulture.

In my circumstances, I seem to be completely disconnected from leisurely things like planting flowers. Strange to say, I unexpectedly had a few months of leisure, but a person accustomed to panting in the rapid currents of life will find such long days boring!

So, I thought of planting some flowers.

Planting flowers is simply a way to dispel that sense of boredom and to spend these months of vague time on those flowers and trees that don't bloom. There is no other meaning. The two plain-colored monthly roses and one white rose were given to me two years ago as a favor by Zen Master Zhiguo. According to Mom, they haven't bloomed in two years and haven't been fertilized in two years. I didn't expect them to still be alive when I returned to my hometown, but they were much more haggard. (The responsibility of the owner!) So, I removed some messy branches and leaves for them, added some fresh soil, and placed them on the fish tank in the courtyard, which turned them into small focal points in this graceful, lonely, empty courtyard.

In addition, there was a white camellia that had just bloomed, a forsythia about to wither, and a wintersweet that had lost all its leaves and flowers. I bought them from the market for more than a dollar. I also turned them into potted plants and placed them in the courtyard with the monthly roses that hadn't bloomed in two years.

But they are all flowers without flowers:

Every morning, I carry a watering can to water them once. Then I move a deck chair next to the flowers, bathe in the spring sunshine, and read a book of Ming dynasty essays or poems that I love. Sometimes, the sound of the fish in the quiet fish tank being sprayed with water, or the "buzzing" of the bees emerging from under the leaves, would take my mind away. I would silently stand up and wander around the flowers for a while, lost in thought looking at the flower shadows of the tassels falling on the water surface and the fish playing under the flower shadows...

Unexpectedly, the weather has turned cold again these past few days.

The white camellia that had just bloomed has been restrained by the cold and has not been able to bloom. The monthly roses and roses that haven't bloomed in two years also show no signs of blooming. Although the wintersweet has sprouted green shoots, it wants us to pin our hopes on winter.

No flowers, no flowers! Last night I listened to the rain all night, and when I got up and ran into the courtyard, I saw that the forsythia flowers that were about to wither had all fallen. Only a spider had spun a web under the flowers, catching a few fallen petals, as if trying to hold back this passing spring.

Spring is over. I was quite moved to travel.

Fire (5) 301

— Fei'er

Besides discussing my ten years of struggle, we also occasionally talked about the recent business conditions in Nanyang. In Nanyang, people must talk about business conditions; there is nothing else to talk about. Gradually, we talked about the local business situation, his own store, and my uncle's. When it came to that, my friend lowered his voice and said solemnly:

"Oh, Yisheng, I think your uncle's business is very dangerous! He certainly earned a lot in the past; he is very good at managing, but he sent most of his earnings back home. I heard that he built a large building in his hometown and bought some land, which is very good. Now, unfortunately, the 'recession' has come. At this moment, it is impossible to get goods without cash. Business at all levels is difficult; no one dares to lend on credit. So, because his coffers are empty, he is really suffering! He almost went bankrupt last year, but fortunately, he had the means to revive it. But the business has already been damaged at its root, and it is even more difficult to sustain under these precarious conditions. Although his store announces that it has made money every year, after actually investigating and researching, it lost at least ten thousand the year before last, and last year was even worse; I'm afraid it was more than twenty thousand? And last year's crisis, although covered up, the emptiness at the center is known to everyone. Businessmen, who doesn't keep their eyes open when doing business? Outwardly strong but inwardly weak will eventually reveal flaws in business, right? So I am always worried about him!"

These words caused me great surprise, as they were completely contrary to what my uncle said every day. And with the prosperity of the Junxing Company signboard ten years ago, it is truly unbelievable that this could be happening. Is it possible that a businessman with means like my uncle is helpless under the iron fist of this "recession"? However, Zhang's words can be trusted. Although they are business rivals, in friendship, what he says to me has always been honest and reliable. Regarding my uncle's building, I visited it when I went home on summer vacation the year before last; I heard it cost fifty or sixty thousand silver dollars to build. So, in any case, this is true. And now, based on my uncle's thin physique and the serious complexion I saw today, this is the best ironclad proof. And today, when I walked through the warehouse, there were very few goods sparsely placed inside. Ten years ago, it was piled full, and we had to rent a native's house to help store them. So, based on these events, the seriousness of the situation is truly worrying. In the midst of it, I exclaimed: "Oh! What to do?"

"But, my friend," my friend said slowly, gently, "Perhaps he has thought of plans that others have not thought of? He was able to turn around last year's crisis; can't he come up with brilliant ideas again now? Previously, he insured the store and goods for one hundred thousand guilders of fire insurance. In these times when cash is very tight, he doesn't even consider the immediate needs, but pays a significant insurance premium, hoping for future safety. This event is truly suspicious! People say that this fox's brilliant plan has arrived!"

I listened in silence, quietly thinking about the reason for this. At this time, it was already dark, and the coconut trees showed their black, huge bodies, standing majestically in this primitive world's night. After a while, the sky was covered with dark clouds, as if it was about to rain. Suddenly, the wind blew again, and I said:

"Let's go back! I'm afraid it will rain!"

"If the wind blows, there won't be any rain. However, it's too dark. Let's go back to the store to sit and talk. I'm afraid they have already come and are waiting for us."

Local Supplement of Shenbao

Talking

Why Bother Going to University? 302

— Mingtang

Recently, George Bernard Shaw had an article called "Why Bother Going to University?" (see translated text in International Translation Report). This topic is very strange. Its content is that modern universities cannot teach people practical knowledge. They can only teach people false knowledge. They can only "first empty your mind, and then fill it with false thoughts" (Shaw's words). Therefore, he opposes universities and modern universities. He wants "all the universities in the world to be razed to the ground and disappear forever" (ibid.). He tells students to throw away all the textbooks in school, because these textbooks are useless and can only harm people. Then you should "sift through the sand to find gold" in a lot of practical knowledge, as if looking for what you want to learn. These things are the real knowledge you want to learn (all Shaw's words).

Why does Shaw so strongly oppose modern universities? He has his reasons. His reason is: "Not long ago, world civilization was almost destroyed by a terrible war. This war was constituted by people with university degrees. There are two truly dangerous people in the world, one is the half-educated, who have destroyed most of civilization; the other is the all-wise and all-powerful intellectual class, who have almost destroyed the entire world. Therefore, he said, "I believe that to preserve a civilization, we need people with some primitive spirit. But the people created by universities mostly have false intelligence." So he had to strongly oppose universities, modern universities. Moreover, he "predicted" that "the collapse of modern civilization is imminent, and the so-called dark age will return to this land." What a painful critique.

However, criticism is just criticism after all. Shaw is just a writer with a great satirical ability. Here, he cannot expose where the fundamental weakness of modern universities lies. Of course, under his pen, his article should be written like this. However, to more thoroughly explain the meaning of this article, we cannot help but give it considerable supplementation. Furthermore, he said that now I need people with some "primitive spirit", which is also wrong. The reason why things are bad is not in whether people are primitive or not, but in the change of the system. Did Shaw clearly point it out? No. Obviously, Shaw is just a satirical writer, just a Fabian liberal, a humanitarian. He does not have a clear understanding of reality.

What is the fundamental reason why modern universities are bad? Shaw only pointed out how bad modern universities are, and we must further point out why they are bad, and then eliminate this badness, which is the right thing to do.

The problem is not whether knowledge is true or false, or whether human emotions are primitive or not, but that the old era has been corrupted and destroyed. We do not ask for primitive spirit, we want to renew the spirit of an era; we do not want to "eliminate" universities, we want a university of another new era; we do not deny education, we want a new education that surpasses the current era.

Mourning a Friend 305

— Yafei

That cruel environment! It actually destroyed my friend and took him away!

This is something worth grieving over. Yesterday, I suddenly received a very unfortunate and heartbreaking report from another friend, Zu. He said, "Yun! Do you know? Ruben has already passed away! This news came from one of his relatives this morning. How tragic is that!"

"Ruben has passed away"! When these words pierced my eardrums, how heartbroken I was! He was not only my good friend but also my only confidant in life. He was currently a revolutionary youth with ambition and new ideas. Alas! Why do good people often not live long? The heartlessness of the azure heavens is truly hateful. At that time, my hands were trembling, shaking as if sifting chaff. One hand gripped the telephone receiver, unable to utter even half a sentence. A cold draft penetrated from my back, through my spine, and into my lungs. Two teardrops fell patteringly, hanging from my cheeks onto my chest. I wished I could rush to see him one last time, but he was far away in Shaoxing, and I certainly couldn't sprout wings and fly over the Qiantang River. I could only shed tears and grieve here!

Ruben, my friend! Please forgive me! We have been together for several years, truly like siblings, but I never expected that now, even seeing you one last time is impossible. Forgive me! I remember saying to you in the past, "Let us share happiness and hardships together, using our two pure hearts, using our two sacred souls, to fight against the environment, to struggle with society, to open up our bright future, to create our new life!" Now, all of this has become a dream. You have left this filthy world and gone to another silent and invisible, pure world. "A coffin encloses the body, and all matters cease!" But of course, my tiny soul has already followed after you; however, my half-stiff body has not yet transformed, it still exists.

Indeed, you previously expressed to me your dissatisfaction with real life and your longing for the illusion of life's annihilation – death. Isn't that so? I also comforted you like this: "In the world, no one will have complete joy. Annihilation, life will eventually come to this one day, but it is only a matter of sooner or later." Unexpectedly, you have now gone before me to practice my words, and you have actually experienced life's annihilation! You are ultimately a brave and extraordinary person. I only have admiration and shame for you!

But I cannot be like this, I definitely cannot be like you; because I have not forgotten the mission that the times have given me! Although the heavy pressure of life refuses to let me go for even a moment, I cannot therefore abandon the responsibilities that life requires.

Do you remember? In the autumn of the year before last, autumn is a touching season. At this time, I was still with you. I casually, no, habitually, talked about my background, and became aware of the current pain. Moreover, at that time, I suffered a major blow, so I was so angry that fire almost came out of my eyes. But, finally, I vomited several mouthfuls of fresh blood because of this. However, I became resolutely aware from then on. From then on, I am not passive, nor do I resent, but I try hard to build the foundation of my life. For three years, although I am still the same, my will has been tempered much more resilient than before. On a dusk intertwined with bleak winds and bitter rain, my body was lying on a hospital bed. Thank you for your kindness, not minding the long journey from Hangzhou to visit me. I am of course very grateful to you, but my heart was indeed extremely painful at that time; I could only mechanically stare at you with two lifeless eyes, without saying anything to you. The reason is that I really couldn't say anything, and I didn't want to say anything to make you sad!

Ruben, my friend! We have known each other for several years, and there has never been any disagreement between us. Although there were sometimes some small misunderstandings, everyone was very understanding, so there was never any deeper quarrel.

This, I should blame you for. Your personality is too stubborn, too unyielding. You fell ill in the autumn of last year, and I advised you to seek medical treatment, but you valued money too much. "If you have money, start with money; if you don't have money, start with your body" is true, you don't have a lot of money, but you have to think of a way! Your illness deepened day by day, and I think it was ultimately not worth it!

Since you went to bed, Zu and I have come to visit you many times. You were sometimes good and sometimes bad, which really worried me. Later, my younger brother, Xiongfei, was falsely imprisoned on January 6th, so I suffered another major blow; I was bedridden for half a month. A few days later, when I came to see you, I didn't expect that you had already been taken away by that Shanghai-Hangzhou train, so I had to return disappointed. After you arrived in the countryside, although I sent you many letters, I didn't receive even one reply.

Now, I suddenly received such an unfortunate message. Alas! Ruben, my friend! Have you carelessly abandoned your friend of many years who was hard to separate from? Ah!

The world is impermanent, leaving only a dusty bed,

Where to find your appearance and voice, sadly gazing at the lute and person.

Misfortune in a Poor Family 307

— Ben

Because I had insomnia the night before, I couldn't muster any energy when I got up early, and my head was dizzy. But for the sake of my job, no, let's put it bluntly, for the sake of "food" to eat, I had to force myself to work. I barely managed to get through three hours until it was time for lunch. After eating, I ran back to the dormitory. It was really a struggle to get my legs and arms up the stairs. Without even wiping my face, and not even thinking about my "not yet quit" smoking addiction, I fell backward onto the bed and fell asleep in less than a minute. However, I didn't sleep peacefully, because it was already twenty minutes past twelve when I went to bed, and I had something to do at one o'clock.

When one o'clock struck, Mr. ×, my roommate, seemed to have called me before going downstairs. I also seemed to have responded in my dream, "I'll get up right away." My body suddenly turned to the side, the clock struck with a clang, and I woke up with a jolt.

At this time, I remembered my great treasure – the fur coat. Because it was a great treasure, I cherished it exceptionally. After taking it off, I would wrap it up carefully. When summer approached, I was even more afraid of insect damage and mildew, so I would take it out and hang it in the sun whenever the sun was in the sky.

On this day, I had hung it on the bamboo pole in front of the window about an hour before my afternoon nap. I knew the wind was blowing quite hard, so I had firmly tied the bamboo pole to the leg of the table inside the room with a rope. That way, I should have been able to rest assured. Moreover, even though I was so sleepy in the afternoon, when I entered the room, I took a look at it, and it was there. Mr. × seemed to have said to me before going downstairs, "The fur coat can be taken in, the wind is blowing too hard."

In this short period of less than ten minutes, my fur coat fell downstairs, and with one fall, it became a theft case.

I was extremely surprised, surprised at the boldness of the theft, probably as big as a "lantern."

When I rolled out of bed, wiped my eyes, and walked to the window, ah! The fur coat was gone! I quickly looked down out the window, but I didn't see it lying on the ground either. I was anxious, so anxious that I ran downstairs and found Mr. ×. Mr. × said that when he went downstairs, my fur coat was clearly there. So I ran to the courtyard facing the windowsill, asking this person, who said he hadn't seen it, and asking that person, who didn't know either.

In this short period of less than ten minutes, the theft of my fur coat was confirmed.

The second floor is the student dormitory, the lower floor is the housing for the school workers, and in front is a school-run stove for boiling water. Usually, when I look out the window at this narrow and desolate courtyard, there are no outsiders. Not a single student ever comes here, and the only people are the workers at the stove shuttling back and forth, the maids washing and drying clothes here, and sometimes one or two other school workers hanging around in a shady way. However, when I went to question these responsible and suspicious personnel, they all denied it outright. Because I am a teacher and they are school workers, I couldn't bear to use some kind of threatening tactic, and others would not sympathize. My fur coat was lost just like that. There was nothing I could do. But how anxious I was!

A coat made of dozens of old foreign dollars was my only property. I had only worn it for two seasons, and it was still half new. I had long had this plan to put a new lining on it in the autumn, so that I could show it off to my friends in the winter. What a good fur coat!

Alas, for the past few days, I have been recalling the purchase of this fur coat, which was the result of so much sweat and effort. Now that it is lost, how terrifying will the winter be, making me unable to rest for a moment. Alas, misfortune in a poor family, suffering this theft, besides swallowing tears, I also have to put my hands together and recite "Amitabha."

Thunder 308

— Luojia

Thunder symbolizes the beginning of a new era. In the scorching summer, not a single cloud can be found in the sky, and the scorching sun radiates thousands of streams of heat. The lush green leaves curl up one by one, appearing very tired. The tiles of people's houses are so dry that they are about to crack, just like a traveler in the desert who desperately needs a sip of cool, clear water. Wild dogs drag their tails, stick out their tongues, and pant in the shade of the wall. People are even more anxious to jump into a pool of clear water to feel comfortable. Everyone's heart is filled with the fear of being scorched to death.

Suddenly, in this unbearable heat, a deafening thunderclap suddenly came in the sky. In an instant, clouds gathered one by one, forming a dark mass, and rain as big as fists, like the Yellow River bursting its banks, poured down on every piece of scorched earth. Flashing lightning and booming thunder played together a piece of the world's most perfect music of power.

After a while, the rain stopped, and the thunder also stopped. The sky was blue, and the earth was moist. The unbearable heat that had been forcing people to death before had been eliminated by the great thunder. Therefore, people's hearts felt an unspeakable comfort and joy, just like coming out of a dark and suffocating cave into a field of fresh air. At this time, everyone thought that they had entered another world suitable for survival, without the fierce flames of the scorching sun, the suffocating air, and the stinging mosquitoes and flies.

Now, we are in this scorching environment.
